 aam aadmi party main andruni ghamaasan jari he
 'AAP' MLA Rajesh Rishi tweeted
 twit main unhone arvind kejariwal par ishaaron hi ishaaron main sawaal khadey kiye hai
 He has written, 'the king in whom pride arises, he sinks his kingdom himself'
 janakapuri se vidhayak rajesh rishi party ke bade netakumar vishwasako tag kar twit kiya
 Rajesh wrote, 'just as bitter medicine cures cancer, similarly a king surrounded by bitter advice and bravado cannot save his existence'
 sutron ke mutabik rajesh rishi apni vidhansabha ke vaardon main tikat ke bantbare se naaraaz hai
 Some candidates are completely ignoring the MLA during campaigning
 janakapuri vidhansabha se vidhayak rajesh rishi ne apane twitor par lagaataar kai twit kiye hai
 He also wrote, 'good days are good as long as we identify and exclude the wrong people hidden in the guise of our loved ones'
 vidhayak ke najdiki sutron ke mutabik rajesh rishi jald hi arvind kejariwal se milane kaa vakt maang sakate hai
 Right now the sharp attitude of the MLA can raise the Aam Aadmi Party's concern just before the start of campaigning in the Delhi Municipal Corporation elections
 chalate-chalate ghatata ja rahaa he AAP kaa kunba!bijepi main shaamil hue vidhayakaisase pehle bavana se aam aadmi party ke vidhayakavedprakash sharmaane bijepi main shaamil hokar aam aadmi party ko bada jhatka diya tha
 After which the discussion about the displeasure of mlas from inside the party was intensified
 bataa den ki aam aadmi party ne 272 siton par ummidavaaron kaa elaan kar diya he
 Also, publicity has started
 shaadi or PM pad par rahul gandhi agar apane fasebuk wal par kuch likhen to usapar kya pratikriya hogi
 Here is the satire courtesy of unreal Times
 (aajtak presents this satire in partnership with the unreal Times) Shyamlal Aggarwal, 70, heads the Odisha Rice Millers Association
 
 
 bargad jile main unki teen rice mil or ek solvent extrection plant (khaadya tel banane vaala plant) he
 His relatives also have many rice mills in the state, yet he says that running rice mills is a loss deal, and it is very difficult to stay in this business
 shyaamalaal agarwal hamen bataate hai, "karmchaariyon ko jo vetan hamen dena padataa he or bijli kaa kharch yaa mil chalaane main jo kharch aata he, uske baad kuch bhi nahin bachataa
 
 
 The milling charge given to us by the government has not been increased for the last 10 years
 
 
 hamaare liye is dhandhe main tike rahanaa aasaan nahin he
 
 
 " agarwal kii is pidaa ke baavjood unka kaarobaar pichley kuch saalon main phala-phula he or unka iraadaa ise chhodane kaa katai nahin he
 Like Agarwal, Jaiprakash Lat of Bargad has also made great progress in the rice business
 vah kehete hai ki unhone mahaz 65 rupee se shuruyaat kii thi or aaj vah kai rice milon ke maalik hai
 He says that business is difficult, but he is working
 "ghaataa yaa pareshaani to kisi bhi dhandhe main hoti he, lekin kaamyaab vahi aadmi hota he, jo bijness ko soch-samajhakar karata he
 
 
 " bargad zile main rajya ke 25 fisadi dhan kii sarkari kharid hoti he
 The number of rice mills continued to grow here in the last few years
 aaj puure rajya main jahaan 1,000 se adhik rice milen hai, vahiin bargarh main pichley ek dashak main inaki sankhya chaar se badhkar 104 ho gai he
 But the irony is that in this barn, farmers have been committing suicide under the burden of debt
 aakhir is virodhabhas kaa sach kya he
 
 
 The The CAG report tabled in Parliament in December says that there were many mistakes in the procurement of paddy between 2009-10 and 2013-14
 
 
 is report se pataa chalata he ki pichley kai saalon main kisaanon kaa haq maaraa gaya or mil maalikon ko najayas phayda pahunchaa
 As an example mil maalikon ko bevajaah dhan dhulaai kii keemat dene se sarkaar ko 195 karod kaa ghaataa hua
 
 
 The government also suffered a loss of 952 crores due to the incorrect scale created about the proportion of rice produced in different states
 
 
 sieji ne report main kaha he ki iskaa pataa nahin ki samarthan mulya ke naam par kisaanon ko di gai 17,985 karod rupee kii rakam asal main un tak pahunchi yaa nahin
 
 
 But the biggest problem is with the three by-products from the paddy, on which the government does not charge any price from the mill owners
 sarkaar mil maalikon ko dhan kii kutai ke liye paisa detii he or dhan kii milling ke vakt usase nikalne vaale teen bai-product bhi mil maalikon ko hi milte hai
 These are by-products
 
 
 rice bran, jisase rifind oil banaaya jaataa he
 
 
 Broken rice or kanki, used for making wine and animal feed
 
 
 rice hask yaa bhusi, jo boyler chalaane yaa bijli banane ke kaam aati he
 
 
 The CAG states in its report - Despite a significant increase in the earnings from the by-product, the government has not changed the milling charge paid to the mill owners since 2005
 isse mil maalikon ko 3,743 karod rupee kaa atirikt phayda hua
 RTI activist Gaurishankar Jain says that he has been complaining to the central and state government in this matter
 gaurishankar jain ne NDTV india se kaha, "meri shikaayat kaa sarkaar ne sangyaan liya or phir ise lekar jo sieji jaanch hui, usamen hazaron karod rupee kii gadabadi kii baat saamne ai he
 The government is not only ignoring the earnings made from rice bran, broken rice and husk for the mill owners for many years, but the mill owners are not paying any income tax on the earnings from these by-products
 
 
 " On the other hand, the mill owners say that if they are in the market then only on the basis of the income from the by-product, because the government has not increased the price of paddy milling for the last several years and even today only Rs 20 per quintal milling
 Get charged
 udhar kisaan kehete hai ki sarkaar is ore dhyaan hi nahin de rahi he
 Barkar farmers JK Sahu and PK Ganapathi say, "mill owners are constantly getting rich
 
 
 is dhandhe main itani kamai ho rahi he ki agar aap bargad ke mil maalikon kaa biodata uthaa len to pataa chalegaa ki jo kuch saal pehle tak maamuli log the, ve aaj na keval mil maalik hai, balki dilli or mumbai jaise mahanagaron main unke paas dher sari sampatti bhi he
 
 
 "comments lekin sarkari adhikari vijay kumaar rath kehete hai ki agar kisaanon ko ghaataa or mil maalikon ko phayda ho rahaa he to yah sirf nitigat gadabadi kii vajah se he
 Our job is to pay the paddy milling money to the mill owners and withdraw 67 percent of the rice from them
 bai-product ke bare main policy main koi vyavastha nahin he
 So, even though policy lapses are responsible for this shortage, it is also true that while mill owners have built a huge empire in Orissa and the entire country, including Bargad, the condition of farmers has worsened everywhere
 shyaamalaal agarwal hamen bataate hai, "karmchaariyon ko jo vetan hamen dena padataa he or bijli kaa kharch yaa mil chalaane main jo kharch aata he, uske baad kuch bhi nahin bachataa
 
 
 The milling charge given to us by the government has not been increased for the last 10 years
 
 
 hamaare liye is dhandhe main tike rahanaa aasaan nahin he
 
 
 " agarwal kii is pidaa ke baavjood unka kaarobaar pichley kuch saalon main phala-phula he or unka iraadaa ise chhodane kaa katai nahin he

 " bargad zile main rajya ke 25 fisadi dhan kii sarkari kharid hoti he

 Barkar farmers JK Sahu and PK Ganapathi say, "mill owners are constantly getting rich
 
 
 is dhandhe main itani kamai ho rahi he ki agar aap bargad ke mil maalikon kaa biodata uthaa len to pataa chalegaa ki jo kuch saal pehle tak maamuli log the, ve aaj na keval mil maalik hai, balki dilli or mumbai jaise mahanagaron main unke paas dher sari sampatti bhi he
 
 
 "comments lekin sarkari adhikari vijay kumaar rath kehete hai ki agar kisaanon ko ghaataa or mil maalikon ko phayda ho rahaa he to yah sirf nitigat gadabadi kii vajah se he
 Our job is to pay the paddy milling money to the mill owners and withdraw 67 percent of the rice from them
 bai-product ke bare main policy main koi vyavastha nahin he
 So, even though policy lapses are responsible for this shortage, it is also true that while mill owners have built a huge empire in Orissa and the entire country, including Bargad, the condition of farmers has worsened everywhere
 misaal ke taur par The government incurred a loss of 195 crores by giving the price of paddy transportation to the mill owners unnecessarily
 
 
 alag-alag rajyon main dhan se nikalne vaale chaaval ke anupaat ke bare main banaae gaye galat paimaane se bhi sarkaar ko 952 karod kaa nuksaan hua
 
 
 The CAG has said in the report that it is not known whether the amount of Rs 17,985 crore given to farmers in the name of support price actually reached them
 
 
 lekin sabase badi gadabadi dhan se nikalne vaale teen bai-products ko lekar he, jin par sarkaar mil maalikon se koi keemat nahin vasuulati
 The government gives money to the mill owners for paddy milling and the mill owners also get three by-products produced during the milling of the paddy
 ye bai-product hai
 
 
 Rice bran, which makes refined oil
 
 
 broken rice yaa kanaki, jo sharaab banane or pashu aahaar ke liye istemaal hota he
 
 
 Rice husk or husk, which is used to run boilers or make electricity
 
 
 sieji apni report main kahati he - bai-product se hone vaali kamai main khaasi badhotaree ke baavjood sarkaar ne mil maalikon ko die jane vaale milling charge ko saal 2005 se abhi tak nahin badla he
 This gave the mill owners an additional Rs 3,743 crore
 artiai kaaryakarta gaurishankar jain kehete hai ki is maamle main vah centre or rajya sarkaar se shikaayat karte rahe hai
 Gourishankar Jain told NDTV India, "the government took cognizance of my complaint and then the CAG investigation related to it has revealed a mess of thousands of crores of rupees
 sarkaar na keval mil maalikon ko rice bran, broken rice or bhusi se hone vaali kamai ko kai saal se andekha kar rahi he, balki mil maalik in bai-products se hone vaali kamai par koi inkam tex bhi nahin de rahe hai
 
 
 " udhar mil maalikon kaa kahana he ki agar ve bazaar main tike hai to keval bai-product se ho rahi aamadani ke dam par, kyonki sarkaar ne pichley kai saal se dhan kii kutai ke daam nahin badaye hai or aaj bhi prati quintal 20 rupee hi milling charge miltaa he
 On the other hand, the farmers say that the government is not paying attention to this
 bargad ke kisaan jeke sahu or pike ganpati kehete hai, "mil maalik to lagaataar amir ho rahe hai
 
 
 This business is earning so much that if you pick up the biodata of Bargad mill owners, then you will find that those who were modest people till a few years ago, they are not only mill owners today, but they have lots in metros like Delhi and Mumbai
 All property is also there
 
 
 "tippaniyan But government official Vijay Kumar Rath says that if the farmers are losing money and the mill owners are benefiting, it is only because of policy disturbances
 hamaara kaam mil maalikon ko dhan milling ke paise dena or unase 67 pratishat chaaval waapas lenaa he
 There is no system in the policy regarding the by-product
 so, bhale hi is kami ke liye nitigat gadabadiyaan zimmedaar hon, lekin yah bhi sach he ki jahaan mil maalikon ne bargad samet urisa or puure desh main ek bada samrajya khadaa kiya he, vahiin kisaanon ke liye haal har jagah kharaab hi hote gaye hai

 Samajwadi Party councilor Rais Sheikh in Mumbai has made a peculiar demand from the Food and Drug Administration (FDA) and the Brihanmumbai Municipal Corporation (BMC)
 unhone epad or biemasi se restaurant ke baahar halaal chinh kaa pradarshan sunishchit karne kaa anurodh kiya he
 Please tell that Halal is a process of animal slaughter which is mandatory for Muslims
 unhone kaha ki aisa kiya janaa chahie taaki musalmaan apane man main andeh ke bina baahar kha saken
 Please tell that Sheikh has not made any such demand for Muslims for the first time
 isse pehle haal hi main unhone kaha tha ki aspataalon me oparation ke vakt muslim marizon kii dadhi na kaati jaae
 He said that i am saying all this after taking medical opinion
 iske liye unhone biemasi ko ek letters likhaa tha
 According to Sheikh, whatever comes under the religious aspect, we should pay attention to it
 unhone samvidhan kaa bhi ullekh kiya or kaha ki samvidhan hamen dharmik reeti-rivaaj ko maanane or na maanane kii swatantraaa detaa he
 Sheikh said that it is not mandatory to remove the beard
 aap ise cover kar sakate hai
 Government hospitals are very insensitive about this
 rais shaikh maanate hai ki dadhi islam kaa ek mahatvapurn hissaa he
 But they themselves do not keep it
 unhone kaha ki aisa nahin he ki har musalmaan dadhi rakhata he
 i am a Muslim, but i do not follow customs
 isliye main nahin rakhata
 He further said that this does not mean that i have no right to talk on this issue
 main un logon ke liye bol rahaa hum, jinka main pratinidhitiv karata hum
 Fog enveloped the national capital on Saturday morning
 kohre kaa sarvaadhik asar railgadiyon ke parichaalan par padaa he
 The operation of about 30 trains has been affected
 adhikariyon ne bataaya ki bhagalpur se dilli aane vaali garibarath express railgadee 22 ghante or alipur daur se dilli aane vaali mahananda express 18 ghanton kii deree se chal rahi he
 Simanchal Express is also running late by 18 hours
 rashtriya rajdhani main shanivaar ko nunatam taapmaana saamaanya se ek degree kam 7
 4 degree Celsius was recorded, while the maximum temperature is likely to be around 17 degree Celsius
 bharat mausam vigyaan vibhaag (iemdi) ke ek adhikari ne bataaya, subah ke samay rajdhani main ghanaa koharaa rahaa or aanshik taur par badal chhaae rahe
 Although the sky will be clear during the day
 subah 8
 At 30 pm, 89 percent humidity was recorded in the atmosphere
 isse pehle, shuukravaar ko dilli kaa adhiktam taapmaana saamaanya se chah degree kam 16
 4 ¬∞ c and a minimum temperature of 7 degrees below normal
 4 degree celsius darj kiya gaya tha
 The Lok Sabha passed the Finance Bill last Wednesday
 isi ke saath hi bajet sambandhi satr 2017-18 kii prakriya puri ho gai
 Since the Finance Bill is a money-related bill, it only needs to be passed by the Lok Sabha, and not required to be passed by the Rajya Sabha
 1 april se shuru ho rahe nae vitt varsh ke saath hi inakam tex se jude kuch khaas niyamon main badlaav ho jayega
 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley also announced several changes in income tax in the budget 2017
 vitt vidheyak main kuch badlaavon ko loksabhaa ne apni manjuuri de di he
 In such a situation, you should also know what is going to change from the new financial year i
e
 April 1
 1
 For income between Rs 2
5 lakh and Rs 5 lakh, the tax will be reduced from 10 per cent to 5 per cent
 haalanki, section 87e ke tahat milane vaali 5000 rupee kii chhot ko ghataakar 2500 rupee kar di gai he
 Not only this, income tax payers whose income is 3
 5 lakh rupee se upar he unke liye koi chhot nahin he
 This would mean that a taxable income of Rs 3 to 5 lakh would save Rs 7,700, while those with taxable income of Rs 5 to 50 lakh would save Rs 12,900
 2
 People with annual income ranging from Rs 50 lakh to Rs 1 crore will have to pay 10 percent surcharge
 (vahiin ek karod rupye salanaa inakam vaale logon ko pehle kii hi tarah 15 pratishat sarcharge dena hoga
 ) 3
 For the convenience of individual taxpayers with an annual income (other than business income) of five lakh rupees, a one-page form will be presented for filing tax returns
 4
 There will be no tax benefit for the assessment year 2018-19 on investment in the Rajiv Gandhi Equity Saving Scheme
 is tex seaving skim kii ghoshnaa vitt varsh 2012-13 main kii gai thi
 The scheme was launched to encourage investors who are investing in the securities market for the first time
 5
 If the undisclosed income or property of more than Rs 50 lakh is found during the search operation, then the Income Tax Officer can reopen the tax cases of the last 10 years
 vartmaan main kar adhikariyon ko pichley chah saal ke dastavejon kii hi chaanbin karne kaa adhikaar hasil he
 Taxpayers who do not file their returns on time may have to pay a fine of up to Rs 10,000 for the assessment year 2018-19
 haalanki, yadi kisi vyakti kii kul aay 5 lakh rupye se adhik nahin he, to is dhara ke tahat us par adhiktam jurmaane kii raashi 1,000 rupye se adhik nahin hogi
 6
 long turm gen ke liye kisi sampatti ke holding period ko 3 saal se ghataakar ab 2 saal kar diya gaya he
 If a person buys property and sells it within 2 years, then he has to pay short term capital gains tax on the profit made on it
 yadi is sampatti kii bikri kharidne kii taarikh se do saal baad kii jaati he to us par koi tex dey nahin hoga
 7
 sarkaar ne kiraaye par ghar dene waalon ke kar laabh main katautee kar di he
 According to the current tax law, after adjusting the rental income for the rented property, the taxpayer can avail tax deduction on the entire interest paid on the home loan
 ab nae niyam ke mutabik khud ke rahane vaale makaan ke liye home lone par byaaj ke bhugtan main 2 lakh rupye par tex katautee kaa laabh milegaa lekin rent par di gai property ke liye karadaata rental inakam edjust karne ke baad prativarsh keval 2 lakh rupye par hi tex laabh hasil kar sakegaa
 An amount of more than two lakh rupees can be carried forward for the next eight assessment years
 8
 a person paying rent of more than Rs 50,000 per month will now have to deduct 5 per cent TDS (source Tax)
 kar visheshgyon kaa maananaa he ki is kadam se aise vyakti jinaki rental inakam bahut adhik he, wo kar ke daayre main aa jaaenge
 This rule will be effective from June 1, 2017
 9
 No tax will be levied on partial withdrawal / withdrawal from National Pension System (NPS)
 prastaavit badlaavon ke anusaar, enpies sabsakribers apane anshdaan kaa 25 pratishat hissaa ritairement se pehle apatkaaleen sthiti main nikaal sakenge
 Remember that at retirement only 40 percent of the total fund is tax free
 10
 From July 1, Aadhaar number will be mandatory for PAN card preparation and income tax filing
 sarkaar ne kaledhan kii rokthaam ke liye nakad lenden kii seemaa bhi 3 se ghataakar ab 2 lakh rupye kar di gai he
 If a person is found to be transacting more than two lakh rupees, then he will have to pay 100 percent penalty for the amount exceeding this limit

 " singh ab ek army ranger ban chuke hai or vah 'bronj star medal' vijeta hai

 bhedbhaav ke mukademe ke baad sena ne unhen disambar main sthaayee taur par isaki ijaajat de di thi

 singh ne dharmik bhedbhaav kaa hawala dete hue mukadmaa daayar kiya tha
 a judge said in the judgment that the army could not pressurize Singh for a personal test
 faisle main sena ko unke aagrah par 31 march tak faisla lene ko bhi kaha gaya
 In a court decision, Singh was finally granted permanent permission on Thursday
 sena main janashakti or rigerv maamalon kii sahaayak sachiv dabra es

 Why it is important to be strong 1
 desh kii sovrain reating par pad saktaa he vipareet asarabite ek saal main mudies, fich or esendpy jaisi global reating agenciyaan kah chuki hai ki aane vaale dinon main bharat ke aarthik aankadon or aarthik sudhaaron kaa asar dikhaai dene par reating main badlaav kiya ja saktaa he

 The farmers of Mandsaur in Madhya Pradesh once again seem to be against the government
 is baar pyaaj or lahasun kii banpar paidaavaar ke baad mandiyon ke baahar kisaan kai- kai din tak upaj bechney kaa intjaar kar rahe hai, to duusari ore pyaaj or lahasun ke bhav main giravat se kisaan ghate main bhi ja rahe hai
 Mandsaur in Madhya Pradesh, famous for the Pashupatinath temple and poppy cultivation, suddenly made headlines around the world when 6 farmers were killed by police bullets during the Kisan agitation and the history of Mandsaur dated June 6, 2017 i became a black spot
 us din madhya pradesh ke malwa ilaake main basaa mandsaur madhya pradesh vidhansabha chunaav ke liye ek raajnneetik prayogshaala ban gaya or iske centre main tha 17 saal kaa yuvak abhishek patidaar
 Abhishek was the first person to die in police firing during the Kisan agitation, but even a year and a half after the accident, Abhishek's mother lamented that the demands on which the agitation took place remain the same
 abhishek kii maa alka patidaar bataati hai ki kisaan andolan main karjamaafee or fasal kaa sahi daam mukhya maang thi, lekin abhi tak donon maangon par sarkaar se sivaay aashwaasan kuch nahin mila
 With a view to pacify the anger of 'bhavantar' from the Bhanwarkisan movement, the Shivraj government started the Bhavantar Yojana, in which the government gives a little more on its behalf above the price of the produce so that the farmer gets more than the price he gets in the market 
 kareeb 70 fisadi kisaan aabaadi vaale mandsaur main kisaanon kii naaraazgi sarkaar ko isliye bhi baari pad sakati he kyonki jin kisaanon ko bhavantar kaa maraham shivaraj sarkaar ne diya tha, us bhavantar ke bhavar main kisaan fansata dikh rahaa he
 Many farmers say that they used to get good prices for their produce before the Bhavantar, but after the Bhavantar the prices of the produce have gone so low in the market that even after adding the amount the farmers are still in loss
 shivaraj sarkaar se naaraaz kisanphilhal mandsaur jile main 4 vidhansabha siten aati hai, jinamein 3 par bijepi kaa kabja he
 But the farmers are angry with the government for not getting the right price for the produce
 mandsaur or uske aasapaas pyaaj or lahasun kii banpar paidaavaar hui he or uske chalate mandsaur krishi upaj mandi ke baahar kai ton pyaaj or lahasun laade tractor-traaliyon kii lambii qatari lag gai he
 Several tons of onions and garlic were found scattered on the ground inside the market
 mandsaur main itnaa pyaaj aa gaya he ki ab kisaanon ko 50 paise prati kilo ke bhav se pyaaj bechnaa pad rahaa he
 a farmer Shyam Patidar said that he sold onions at the rate of 50 paise per kg on November 20 and incurred a loss of five and a half rupees on every kg
 sirf pyaaj hi nahin balki lahasun kii girti keemton ne bhi kisaanon ke saamne dohari musiibat khadi kar di he
 The farmer cannot keep garlic for more than 3-4 days, so even after getting a low price, he is compelled to sell garlic in compulsion
 ghate main kisanmandsaur kii mandi main madhya pradesh ke ashta, sihor, bhopal or ujjain jile ke alaava rajasthan ke bansawada or pratapgarh se lahasun aata he jabaki neemuch or rajasthan se pyaaj kii aavak hoti he
 It costs Rs 5-6 to grow one kg of onions, but in Mandsaur Mandi, onion is being sold at the rate of 50 paise per kg
 yani har ek kilo par kisaan ko 4
 Losses range from 50 rupees to 5 rupees
 duusari ore, ek quintal lahasun ugane main 3000 rupye kaa kharch he, lekin mandsaur mandi main lahasun 700 rupye prati quintal ke bhav se bik rahaa he
 That is, the farmer is at a loss of 2300 rupees for every quintal of garlic
 beete ek saptaah main lagbhag 1 lakh 20 hajaar bori pyaaj or lagbhag itani hi bori lahasun mandsaur mandi main aa chukaa he
 The demand for punishment of the accused is considered very important by the Patidars votebank in Mandsaur located at one end of Malwa
 kisaan andolan main sabase sakriy bhoomika nibhaane vaale kisaan netaa amritraam patidaar bataate hai ki mandsaur main 16 fisadi patidaar hai, jo puri tarah se sarkaar badalane kaa man bana chuke hai
 According to Amritram Patidar, the farmers are angry that neither the debt of the farmers was waived after the Kisan agitation nor the convicts of the firing
 netaaon ke apane tarksthaneey vidhayak or bijepi pratyaashee yashpal singh sisodiya ne bhavantar ke bhugtan main deree or fasal ke kam daam kaa dosha congress par daal diya

 isiilie hamaara mantra he 'meraa booth - sabase majboot' : piem modi - The opportunity to punish the Congress which has enmity with Madhya Pradesh and its people has come to the people of Madhya Pradesh: PM Modi - piem modi ne kaha ki jo party 125 saalon se bhi puraani ho, jis party ke anekon bhootpurv rajyapal ho, phir aisa kya hua itani badi party ko sookshmdarshi yantra lekar nikalnaa padataa he ki desh main kahin bache hai kii nahin or itani paraajay ke baad bhi congress sudharne ko taiyaar nahin he
 - PM Modi said that the realization of forward and backward in Madhya Pradesh will not do good to the country - jab tak dilli main upie kii sarkaar thi tab tak wo bhaajapa kii rajya sarkaron or vahaan kii janata ke prati dushmani kaa bhav paalkar baithe the : piem modi - PM Modi said that we fight elections not with money force but with manpower
 - ham wo log he jinhen gandhi bhi manjuur he, ram manohar lohia bhi manjuur he or dinadayal upaadhyaay bhi manjuur he kyonki ham samanvay, saamaajik nyaay or sabakaa saath, sabakaa vikaas main vishwaas karte hai : piem modi - The politics of vote bank in our country has destroyed the society like a termite and therefore if the ruin that came in the 70 years of independence is to save the country, then in front of us this country is liberated from the termites of vote bank politics This is the special responsibility of BJP: PM Modi - saath sabakaa vikaas ye sirf chunavi naaraa nahin he
 For a brighter India, it is our path of thoughtful choice to fulfill the Indian hope and aspirations: PM Modi - piem modi ne kaha kipundit deen dayaal upaadhyaay ji kaa chintan, unka jivan, unke aachaar, unke vichaar aaj bhi hamaari prerana he
 - PM Modi said that we all owe debt to thousands of activists who have sacrificed their lives for our great leaders and party and we will not let any opportunity to repay this debt
 - piem modi ne kaha ki aazaadee ke baad desh teen mahapurushon ko kabhi bhul nahin saktaa mahatma gandhi, lohia or pandit dinadayal upaadhyaay; ye teenon desh ko nai oonchaaiyon par le gaye
 -PM Modi said- BJP is the only party that deals with the issue of humanity in political life - bijepi kii 19 rajyon main sarkaar hona garv kii baat he lekin vishwa kii sabase badi party hona usase bhi garv kii baat he : piem modi - How fortunate we are or how many virtues we may not have known that we have got the privilege of serving Maa Bharati through this party (BJP): PM Modi - piem modi ne kaha ki mujhe urja se bhare lakhon log najar aa rahe hai
